void minscanf(const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    char *p;
    int *ip;
    double *dp;
    
    va_start(ap, fmt);
    
    for (p = fmt; *p; p++) {
        if (*p != '%') {
            continue;

            case 'd':
                ip = va_arg(ap, int *);
                scanf("%d", ip);
                break;
            case 'f':
                dp = va_arg(ap, double *);
                scanf("%lf", dp);
                break;
            default:
                break;
        }
    }

}

```c
void minscanf(const char *format, ...)
{
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, format);

    while (*format)
    {
        if (*format == '%')
        {
            format++;
            switch (*format)
            {
                case 'd':
                    {
                        int *num = va_arg(args, int*);
                        scanf("%d", num);
                        break;
                    }
                case 'f':
                    {
                        double *num = va_arg(args, double*);
                        scanf("%lf", num);
                        break;
                    }
                case 's':
                    {
                        char *str = va_arg(args, char*);
                        scanf("%s", str);
                        break;
                    }
                default:
                    break;
            }
        }

        format++;
    }

    va_end(args);
}
```

Received response: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

void minscanf(const char *format, ...) {
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, format);
    
    while (*format) {
        if (*format == '%') {
            switch (*(++format)) {
                case 'd':
                    // Read integer input and assign to a variable
                    int *intPtr;
                    intPtr = va_arg(args, int*);
                    scanf("%d", intPtr);
                    break;
                case 'f':
                    // Read float input and assign to a variable
                    float *floatPtr;
                    floatPtr = va_arg(args, float*);
                    scanf("%f", floatPtr);
                    break;
                case 'c':
                    // Read character input and assign to a variable
                    char *charPtr;
                    charPtr = va_arg(args, char*);
                    scanf(" %c", charPtr);
                    break;
                case 's':
                    // Read string input and assign to a variable
                    char *strPtr;
                    strPtr = va_arg(args, char*);
                    scanf(" %s", strPtr);
                    break;
                default:
                    break;
            }
        }
        format++;
    }
    
    va_end(args);
}

int main() {
    int num;
    float fnum;
    char letter;

```c
if (*format == '%') {
    // handle format specifiers
    if (*(format + 1) == 'd') {
        int *n = va_arg(args, int *);
        scanf("%d", n);
``` 

```c
switch (fmt[0]) {
    case '%':
        handle_formats(&fmt[1], ap);
        break;

    default:
        token = fmt;
        while (*fmt && !isspace(*fmt))
            fmt++;
        handle_string(token, fmt - token);
        break;
}
```

In this default case, we first identify the token by iterating over the characters in `fmt` until we reach a whitespace character. Once we have identified the token, we pass it to a function `handle_string()` along with the length of the token to process it accordingly.

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

void minscanf(const char *format, ...)
{
    va_list ap;
    char *p, *sval;
    int *ival;
    unsigned int *uval;
    double *dval;

    va_start(ap, format);
    for (p = format; *p; p++) {
        if (*p != '%') {
            continue;
        }

        switch (*++p) {
            case 'd':
                ival = va_arg(ap, int *);
                scanf("%d", ival);
                break;
            case 'u':
                uval = va_arg(ap, unsigned int *);
                scanf("%u", uval);
                break;
            case 'f':
                dval = va_arg(ap, double *);
                scanf("%lf", dval);
                break;
            case 's':
                sval = va_arg(ap, char *);
                scanf("%s", sval);
                break;
            default:
                break;
        }
    }
    va_end(ap);
}
```

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

void minscanf(const char *format, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, format);

    const char * arg_p = format;

    // Loop through the format string
    while (*arg_p) {
        if (*arg_p != '%') {
            // Handle regular characters
            if (*arg_p == ' ') {
                // Skip whitespace
                while (isspace(*arg_p)) {
                    ++arg_p;
                }
            }
            else {
                // Match non-whitespace characters
                char ch = getchar();
                if (*arg_p != ch) {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        else {
            // Handle format specifiers
            switch (*(++arg_p)) {
                case 'd': {
                    int *n = (int*) va_arg(ap, int*);
                    scanf("%d", n);
                    break;
                }
                case 's': {
                    char *s = va_arg(ap, char*);
                    char buffer[100];
                    scanf("%s", buffer);
                    strcpy(s, buffer);
                    break;
                }
                default:
                    break;
            }
        }
        ++arg_p;
    }

    va_end(ap);
}

int main() {
    int num;
    char str[100];
    minscanf("%d %s", &num, str);
    printf("Integer: %d, String: %s\n", num, str);

    return 0;
}
```
